< review>
Mr. Chetan Tanna is an experienced and capable immigration lawyer. He helped us immensely to solve several difficult matters with our case and because of him we got through it with no issue at all. The application process is difficult to take on by yourself, just one or two mess ups could cause serious delay or a refusal for your immigration application. That is something that should not be risked, not in today‚Äôs immigration environment. This is the reason a good lawyer is necessary.

Often when we had concerns that were troubling us, Chetan was always available even after business hours. < Review>
If any part of their technology fails, they don't have the capability to execute any sort of contingency plan.

Customer has a as valid coupon.
Sorry, our scanning machine is down.
Okay, can you still honor the coupon?
No, I can't scan it.
Right, but we can read what the coupon says, and I have a calculator built into my phone...I also have cash money.
Our system is down, we can't use coupons.

I'm not sure if this is a bad on corporate subway, or just the local level management. There really needs to be a foolproof way to allow a coupon to be used when a part of the coupon reading technology fails.

Also they leave a little stem part in the jalapenos, but that's not really a big deal.< /Review>

this RV park, needs a lot of work, management often turns off the water, and electricity to work on the property. Management doesn‚Äôt provide maintenance to the property you have to clean and buy your own products to get rid of the weeds, any issue you have to text management they answer whenever they want. Park is in a dirt road which is not very accessible, if cars come out speeding you have to be careful since is only one road in and out. < Review>
I purchased my HVAC system from Canoga Park heating and A/C a while ago and they have kept it running perfectly for many years. Of course, after over ten years of no problems, my A/C decided to have a system malfunction, at night, while the weather reports were predicting 100 plus temperatures in two days. I called Canoga Park Heating and A/C in the morning and to my surprise, not only could they come that day, but they would be there by 1pm. We followed their app, knew who was coming and could tell  how far away Kevin was and when he arrived at the house... so we could mask up!  Kevin quickly found the problem, told me the approx. cost, but said it required  parts that might not be in stock. He asked for a minute to check and came back to tell me, not only were the parts in the warehouse, but they were less expensive than he thought. YAY! Then he told me he could pick up the parts first thing in the morning, but had to check the schedule and I should call, if I hadn't heard back by 3pm. I am so sorry I don't remember the name of the woman I spoke to, because she was wonderful. Kevin, our super hero,  arrived the next morning, fixed the system in record time and just as the temperature started to rise outside.....The temperature  inside was coming down. I would say that this was the most stress free emergency service I've ever experienced.
